<script type="text/javascript">
			//<![CDATA[
			var t2;
			$(function() {
				$('#kereso_fokat_hidden').val('');
				$('#kereso_alkat_hidden').val('');

				text_q = $('#text_q').val();
				text_q_default = 'Alkatrész neve vagy teljes cikkszáma';
				if (!text_q) {
					setTimeout("$('#text_q').val('" + text_q_default + "')", 500);
				}

				$('.helper').click(function(e) {
					var src = $(this).find('img').attr("src");
					var text = $(this).find('span');
					if (src.indexOf('_on') > 0) {
						src = src.replace("_on", "_off");
						setCookie('help', 'off', 365, '/', '.autoalkatresz.hu');
						text.html('Súgó bekapcsolása');
						disableQtips();
					} else {
						src = src.replace("_off", "_on");
						setCookie('help', 'on', 365, '/', '.autoalkatresz.hu');
						text.html('Súgó kikapcsolása');
						createHelpersQtip();
						if ($('#kereso_gyartmany').val() < 1)
							$('#kereso_gyartmany').qtip('show');
					}

					$(this).find('img').attr("src", src);

					e.preventDefault();
				});

				$('#text_q').live('keyup', function(e) {
					$('#kereso_fokat_hidden').val('');
					$('#kereso_alkat_hidden').val('');

					var ascii = e.which || e.charCode;

					if (ascii !== 38 && ascii !== 40 && ascii !== 13 && ascii !== 27) {
						$('#text_q_autocompleter').hide();
						if ($(this).val().length > 2) {
							clearTimeout(t2);
							t2 = setTimeout("textSearch()", 300); // kesleltetjuk
						}
					} else if (ascii == 27) {
						$('#text_q_autocompleter').hide();
						e.preventDefault();
					}
				});

				$('#text_q').live("click", function() {
					if ($(this).val() == text_q_default) {
						$(this).val('');
					}
				});

				$(document).bind("click", function(e) {
					if ($(e.target).attr('id') !== "#text_q_autocompleter" && $(e.target).parents("#text_q_autocompleter").length == 0) {
						$('#text_q_autocompleter').hide();
					}
				});

			});
			//]]>
</script>

	<script type="text/javascript">
		//<![CDATA[
		var jQf = new $.jQForm({debug: false, formObject: "customForm", matchSelectClass: "big"});

		var t;
		$(function() {
			if ($('#akku_dimenzio').length > 0) {
				$('#akku_dimenzio').on("change", function() {
					_obj = $(this);
					if (_obj.val() != 0) {
						$.getJSON('/ajax/akkumulator_meret', {meret: _obj.val(), jkat: 'sz'}, function(data) {
							$('#kereso_meret_hosszusag').val(data.meret.hosszusag);
							$('#kereso_meret_szelesseg').val(data.meret.szelesseg);
							$('#kereso_meret_magassag').val(data.meret.magassag);
						});
					} else {
						$('#kereso_meret_hosszusag').val('');
						$('#kereso_meret_szelesseg').val('');
						$('#kereso_meret_magassag').val('');
					}
					return false;
				});
			}

			setTimeout("resizeBoxes();", 100);
			//resizeBoxes();

			$('.rootCateg a').click(function(e) {
				if ($('.categSubItems').length === 0)
					return true;

				id = $(this).parent().attr("id");

				$('.categSubItems').hide();

				$('.kategorialista_bottom').find('div.rootCateg').each(function() {
					if ($(this).attr("id") !== id) {
						$(this).children().removeClass("collapse");
						$(this).removeClass("opened");
					}
				});

				if (!$(this).hasClass('collapse')) {
					sub = $(this).parent().next();
					h = sub.height();

					//_left = $('#kategorialista_bottom table tr td:eq(0)').width();
					_left = 0;
					switch ($(this).parent().parent().parent().index()) {
						case 1:
							_left = $(this).parent().parent().position().left; //$('#kategorialista_bottom table tr td:eq(0)').width();
							break;

						case 2:
							_left = $(this).parent().parent().position().left; //$('#kategorialista_bottom table tr td:eq(0)').width()+$('#kategorialista_bottom table tr td:eq(1)').width();
							break;
					}

					sub.css({top: '-' + (h + 27) + 'px', left: '-' + _left + 'px'});
					sub.toggle();
				}

				$(this).toggleClass('collapse');
				$(this).parent().toggleClass('opened');

				var obj = $(this);

				e.preventDefault();
			});

			$('.tooltip_close').click(function() {
				$(this).parent().hide();
				$('.kategorialista_bottom').find('div, a').removeClass('collapse');
				$('.kategorialista_bottom').find('div').removeClass('opened');
			});

			$(document).bind("click", function(e) {
				if (!$(e.target).hasClass('rootCateg') && $(e.target).parents().filter('div.rootCateg').length < 1) {
					obj = $('a.collapse');
					obj.click();
				}
			});

	
					/* $('#searchContainerMore').click(function() {
				 window.location = '/alkatresz/reszletes';
				 }); */
				$("#searchContainerMore").live("click", function(e) {
					$('#searchForm').attr("action", "/alkatresz/reszletes");
					$('#text_q').val('');
					$('#searchForm').submit();
					e.preventDefault();
				});
	
				var jkatClicked = 0;
			var gyartmanyClicked = 0;
			$("#kereso_gyartmany").live("change", function(e) {
				select = $('#keresomodell');
				var options = '<option value="0">mindegy</option>';
				if ($(this).val() > 0) {
					data = $('#searchForm').serialize(true);
					$.post('/ajax/modell_lista', data, function(data) {
						$.each(data, function(key, obj) {
							var id = 0;
							for (x in obj) {
								if (id < 1)
									id = x;
							}
							text = obj[x];

							options += '<option value="' + id + '">' + text + '</option>';
						});

						select.html(options);
						$.jQForm.updateSelect(select);

	
						gyartmanyClicked++;
					});
					//console.log($('#ui-tooltip-0 ui-icon ui-icon-close'));
					//$('#kereso_gyartmany').qtip('hide');
					$('#ui-tooltip-kereso-gyartmany').fadeOut('slow');
	
				} else {
					select.html(options);
					$.jQForm.updateSelect(select);
					$.jQForm.closeAllOtherSelects();
					$('#kereso_evjarat_item_0').click();

					if (getCookie('help') == 'on') {
						//ideQtips();
						$('#kereso_gyartmany').qtip('show');
					}

				}
			});

			$('#keresomodell').live('change', function() {
				if ($(this).val() !== "0") {

					} else {
					if (getCookie('help') == 'on' && $('#kereso_gyartmany').val() > 0) {
						$('#keresomodell').qtip('show');
					}
				}
			});


			$("#keresojkat").change(function(e) {
				data = $('#searchForm').serialize(true);
				//console.log(data);
				// reset the model select
				$("#kereso_gyartmany").html('<option value="0">mindegy</option>');
				$("#keresomodell").html('<option value="0">mindegy</option>');
				$("#keresoevjarat_item_0").click();
				$.jQForm.updateSelect($("#keresomodell"));

				$.post('/ajax/gyartmany_lista', data, function(data) {
					select = $('#kereso_gyartmany');

					var options = '<option value="0">mindegy</option>';

					$.each(data, function(key, val) {
						//alert(key + ' - ' + val);
						if (typeof val === 'object') {
							options += '<optgroup label="' + key + '">';
							$.each(val, function(key2, val2) {
								options += '<option value="' + key2 + '">' + val2 + '</option>';
							});
							options += '</optgroup>';
						} else {
							options += '<option value="' + key + '">' + val + '</option>';
						}
					});

					select.html(options);
					//console.log(select.html());
					$.jQForm.updateSelect(select);

	
					jkatClicked++;

					if ($('#kereso_gyartmany').val()>0) {
						hideQtips();
						$('#kereso_gyartmany').qtip('show');
					}

					$.jQForm.closeAllOtherSelects();
				});
			});
	
			if ($("#searchForm").length > 0) {
				t = setTimeout("hirdetes_darabszam()", 800); // kesleltetjuk

				$("#searchForm").find('select, input:checkbox, input:hidden').live("change", function() {
					clearTimeout(t);
					t = setTimeout("hirdetes_darabszam()", 800); // kesleltetjuk
				});

				$("#searchForm").find('input').live('keydown', function() { // keypress backspace nem volt jo
					clearTimeout(t);
					t = setTimeout("hirdetes_darabszam()", 800); // kesleltetjuk
				});

			}

					createHelpersQtip();
	
			});

		var qtipShow = false;

		function createHelpersQtip() {
			$('#kereso_gyartmany').qtip({
				id: 'kereso-gyartmany',
				content: {
					title: {text: 'Márka kiválasztása', button: 'Bezárás'},
					text: 'Milyen jármű márkához keres alkatrészt?'

				},
				position: {
					my: 'left center',
					at: 'right bottom',
					adjust: {
						x: 6
					}
				},
				style: {
					tip: {
						corner: true,
						border: false,
						width: 48,
						height: 15
					},
					classes: 'ui-tooltip-yellow ui-tooltip-rounded'
				},
				show: false,
				hide: false,
				events: {
					hide: function(event, api) {
						$(this).fadeOut('slow');
						disableQtips();
						$('.helper').click();
					},
					show: function(event, api) {
						$('.qtip').hide();
					},
				}
			});

			}
		function resizeBoxes() {
			if (!$('#elhelyezkedesBox').length || !$('#extrakBox').length) {
				return;
			}

			elhelyezkedes_h = parseInt($('#elhelyezkedesBox').css('height').replace('px', ''));
			extra_h = parseInt($('#extrakBox').css('height').replace('px', ''));

			if (extra_h > elhelyezkedes_h) {
				$('#elhelyezkedesBox').css({'height': extra_h});
				$('#extrakBox').css({'height': extra_h});
			} else if (elhelyezkedes_h > extra_h) {
				$('#extrakBox').css({'height': elhelyezkedes_h});
				$('#elhelyezkedesBox').css({'height': elhelyezkedes_h});
			}

		}
		//]]>

	</script>

			var params = { menu: "false",wmode:"transparent" };

	</div>	<script type="text/javascript">
		//<![CDATA[

		$(function() {
			initScroll();
		});

		var direction = 'down';
		var scroll = 0;
		//var scrollMax = Math.ceil($('#smskiemelt').find('li').length / 2) * 83 - parseInt($('#smskiemelt').css('height')) + 10 /* kicsit maradjon lent */;
		scrollMax = parseInt($('#smskiemelt').find('ul').height() - 200) - Math.ceil($('#smskiemelt').find('li').length / 5);
		var scrollingId = false; // timer

		function initScroll() {
			scrollTo();


			$('#smskiemelt').on('mouseover', function() {
				clearInterval(scrollingId);
			});

			$('#smskiemelt').on('mouseout', function() {
				clearInterval(scrollingId);
				scrollingId = setInterval(scrollTo, 40);
			});

			$('#smskiemelt').on('scroll', function() {
				scroll = $(this).scrollTop();
			});
		}

		function scrollTo() {
			scroll = direction === 'down' ? scroll + 1 : scroll - 1;

			if (scroll < 0) {
				scroll = 0;
				direction = 'down';
			} else if (scroll > scrollMax) {
				scroll = scrollMax;
				direction = 'up';
			}

			$('#smskiemelt').scrollTop(scroll);

			clearInterval(scrollingId);
			scrollingId = setInterval(scrollTo, 40);

		}
		//]]>

	</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	//<![CDATA[

	$(function() {
		$('.kategorialista_bottom').hide();
		$('.kategorialista_bottom').each(function(i) {
			head = $(this).prev();
			head.on('click', {'index': i}, openbottomCateg);
			head.css({'cursor': 'pointer'});
		});

		obj = $('.kategorialista_bottom')[0];
		$(obj).show();
		$(obj).prev().find("span").addClass('expand_icon_on');
		$(obj).prev().find("span").removeClass('expand_icon_off');
	});

	function openbottomCateg(e) {
		$('.kategorialista_bottom').each(function(i) {
			if (i == e.data.index) {
				return;
			}

			$(this).prev().find('span').addClass('expand_icon_off');
			$(this).prev().find('span').removeClass('expand_icon_on');
			$(this).hide();
		});

		obj = $('.kategorialista_bottom').eq(e.data.index);
		if (obj.prev().find('h1').find('span').hasClass('expand_icon_on')) {
			obj.hide();
			obj.prev().find('h1').find('span').addClass('expand_icon_off');
			obj.prev().find('h1').find('span').removeClass('expand_icon_on');
		} else {
			obj.show();
			obj.prev().find('h1').find('span').addClass('expand_icon_on');
			obj.prev().find('h1').find('span').removeClass('expand_icon_off');
		}
	}
//]]>
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	//<![CDATA[
	$(function() {
		var jQf2 = new $.jQForm({debug: false, formObject: "userlogin", matchSelectClass: "medium"});

		$('.numeric').keypress(function(event) {

			var keyCode = event.keyCode;
			if (keyCode == 0)
				keyCode = event.which;
			if (!document.all) {
				if (event.charCode == null || event.charCode == 0) {
					return true;
				}
			}
			if ((keyCode >= 48 && keyCode <= 57) || (keyCode == 44) || keyCode == 45) {
				return true;
			} else {
				return false;
			}
		})

		// positive integer, no: ,/-
		$('.numeric_int').keypress(function(event) {

			var keyCode = event.keyCode;
			if (keyCode == 0)
				keyCode = event.which;
			if (!document.all) {
				if (event.charCode == null || event.charCode == 0) {
					return true;
				}
			}

			if ((keyCode >= 48 && keyCode <= 57)) {
				return true;
			} else {
				return false;
			}
		})

	});
	//]]>
</script>
